[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The Jazzer fuzzer detected and prevented a Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Observations and Findings  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace shows that during `[0m[1;35mZipFile.readCentralDirectoryEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` the [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Important Observations  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The code conditionally downloads content if the ZIP comment looks like a URL. [0m [2m                [0m
